</script></center></div><h1 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline">Five Letter Words: 660+ Common 5 Letter Words in English</h1>			</header>
			
		<div class="entry-content" itemprop="text">
			<p>A 5 letter word is one of the most common lengths of <a href="https://7esl.com/words/">words</a> in the English language. There are so many 5 letter words out there for us to choose from and we couldn&#8217;t possibly cover them all here today, but we&#8217;ll try our best to see what we can get through.</p>

<h3><span class="ez-toc-section" id="What_Are_5_Letter_Words"></span>What Are 5 Letter Words?<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>
<p>5 letter words can come in all kinds of different forms, no two words would ever end up meaning the same thing. Whether it&#8217;s a noun you&#8217;re looking for, or maybe a verb, there will always be a 5 letter word available to you!</p><div class="advads-in-article-1" id="advads-733056370"><script type="rocketlazyloadscript" async src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js"></script>
